		bel_slot IO0: legacy;
		bel_slot IO1: legacy;
		bel_slot IO2: legacy;

		bel_slot PICTEST1: legacy;
		bel_slot PICTEST2: legacy;

		tile_class IO_W {
			cell CELL0;

			bel IO0 {
				input CE = IMUX_CE0;
				input CLK = IMUX_CLK0;
				input DEL0 = IMUX_D4;
				input DEL1 = IMUX_C4;
				input DEL2 = IMUX_B4;
				input DEL3 = IMUX_A4;
				output DI = OUT_F0;
				output IPOS0 = OUT_F2;
				output IPOS1 = OUT_F3;
				input LSR = IMUX_LSR0;
				input ONEG0 = IMUX_D0;
				input ONEG1 = IMUX_D2;
				input ONEG2 = IMUX_C0;
				input OPOS0 = IMUX_B0;
				input OPOS1 = IMUX_B1;
				input OPOS2 = IMUX_A0;
				output QNEG0 = OUT_Q2;
				output QNEG1 = OUT_Q3;
				output QPOS0 = OUT_Q0;
				output QPOS1 = OUT_Q1;

		tile_class CONFIG {
			cell CELL0;
			cell CELL1;
			cell CELL2;

			bel START {
				input STARTCLK = CELL0.IMUX_CLK0;
			}

			bel OSC {

			}

			bel JTAG {
				input IJTAGEN = CELL0.IMUX_CE2;

				output JTDI = CELL0.OUT_Q5;
				input JTDO1 = CELL0.IMUX_A1;
				input JTDO2 = CELL0.IMUX_A0;
				output JUPDATE = CELL0.OUT_F6;
			}

			bel GSR {
				input CLK = CELL2.IMUX_CLK1;
				input GSR = CELL0.IMUX_B1;
			}

			bel SED {
				output SEDCLKOUT = CELL0.OUT_Q7;
				output SEDDONE = CELL0.OUT_Q2;
				input SEDENABLE = CELL0.IMUX_CLK1;

				input A3 = CELL0.IMUX_D4;

		tile_class DQS_W {
			cell CELL0;

			bel DQS0 {
				input CLK = IMUX_CLK0;
				output DATAVALID = OUT_Q4;
